namespace = company

#Manage Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.0
	title = "company.0.t"
	desc = "company.0.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {   #Found a new company
		name = "company.0.a" 
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		country_event = { id = company.10 }
	}
	option = {   #Manage existing company
		name = "company.0.b" 
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = india_private_company
				has_country_flag = india_official_company
				has_country_flag = indonesia_private_company
				has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
				has_country_flag = china_private_company
				has_country_flag = china_official_company
				has_country_flag = japan_korea_private_company
				has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
				has_country_flag = persia_private_company
				has_country_flag = persia_official_company
				has_country_flag = south_africa_private_company
				has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
				has_country_flag = east_africa_private_company
				has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
				has_country_flag = west_africa_private_company
				has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
				has_country_flag = indochina_official_company
				has_country_flag = indochina_private_company
				has_country_flag = west_europe_official_company
				has_country_flag = west_europe_private_company
				has_country_flag = west_mediterraneansea_official_company
				has_country_flag = west_mediterraneansea_private_company
				has_country_flag = central_europe_official_company
				has_country_flag = central_europe_private_company
				has_country_flag = balticsea_official_company
				has_country_flag = balticsea_private_company
				has_country_flag = eastern_europe_official_company
				has_country_flag = eastern_europe_private_company
				has_country_flag = tartary_official_company
				has_country_flag = tartary_private_company
				has_country_flag = near_east_official_company
				has_country_flag = near_east_private_company
			} 
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		country_event = { id = company.4 }
	}
	option = {   #Hide Trading Company events
		name = "company.0.c" 
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
			ai = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = hide_tc_event
	}
	option = {   #Show Trading Company events
		name = "company.0.d1" 
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = hide_tc_event
			ai = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
			clr_country_flag = hide_tc_event
	}
	option = {   #Exit
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		name = "company.exit" 
	}

}

#Found Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.10
	title = "company.1.t"
	desc = "company.1.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Found india company
                     name = "company.1.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
                                             has_country_flag = india_official_company
											 has_country_flag = india_private_company
                                   } 
                                   NOT = {
                                             capital_scope = { 
                                             superregion = india_superregion
                                             }
                                   } 
                                   any_owned_province = {
                                             superregion = india_superregion
                                             has_port = yes
                                   }
                                   treasury = 100
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 10
                              modifier = {
                                         factor = 0
                                         NOT = { treasury = 200 }
                              }
		     }
                     set_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     country_event = { id = company.11 }
        }
        option = {   #Found indochina company
                     name = "company.1.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {

#Found Trading Company - official or private
country_event = {
        id = company.11
	title = "company.11.t"
	desc = "company.11.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Found official company
                     name = "company.11.a" 
                     custom_tooltip = company.11.at
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
		     }
                     set_country_flag = found_official_company
                     country_event = { id = company.12 }
        }
        option = {   #Found private company
                     name = "company.11.b" 
                     custom_tooltip = company.11.bt
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
		     }
                     set_country_flag = found_private_company
                     country_event = { id = company.12 }
        }
        option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indonesia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_china_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_japan_korea_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_persia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_east_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_south_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_west_africa_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_west_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_west_mediterraneansea_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_central_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_balticsea_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_eastern_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_tartary_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_near_east_company_1 
                     country_event = { id = company.10 }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
        }
        option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indonesia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_china_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_japan_korea_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_persia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_east_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_south_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_west_africa_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_west_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_west_mediterraneansea_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_central_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_balticsea_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_eastern_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_tartary_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_near_east_company_1
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
        }

}

#Found Trading Company - Initial Funding
country_event = {
        id = company.12
	title = "company.12.t"
	desc = "company.12.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund 100 ducat
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          treasury = 400
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -100
                     set_country_flag = fund_100
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Fund 200 ducat
                     name = "company.fund200" 
                     trigger = { 
                              treasury = 200
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          NOT = { treasury = 400 }
                              }
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          treasury = 1000
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -200
                     set_country_flag = fund_200
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Fund 500 ducat
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = { 
                              treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
                              }
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          treasury = 2000
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -500
                     set_country_flag = fund_500
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Fund 1000 ducat
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = { 
                              treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -1000
                     set_country_flag = fund_1000
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Return
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_official_company
                     clr_country_flag = found_private_company
                     country_event = { id = company.11 }
        }
        option = {   #Exit
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1

                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_200 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = tartary_company_cash value = 200 } 
                            }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_500 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = tartary_company_cash value = 500 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_1000 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = tartary_company_cash value = 1000 }
                            }
                     }
					 if = {
                            limit = { has_country_flag = found_near_east_company_1 }
                            set_country_flag = near_east_company
							set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = near_east_company_size value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_total_balance value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_total_expense value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_total_income value = 0 }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = found_official_company
                                    }
                                    set_country_flag = near_east_official_company
                            }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = found_private_company
                                    }
                                    set_country_flag = near_east_private_company
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_100 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 100 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_200 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 200 } 
                            }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_500 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 500 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_1000 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 1000 }
                            }
                     }
                     #Clear Setup
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indonesia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_china_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_japan_korea_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_persia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_east_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_south_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_west_africa_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_west_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_west_mediterraneansea_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_central_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_balticsea_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_eastern_europe_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_tartary_company_1
					 clr_country_flag = found_near_east_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_official_company
                     clr_country_flag = found_private_company
                     clr_country_flag = fund_100 
                     clr_country_flag = fund_200

###Trading Company Upgrade
province_event = {
    id = company.21
	title = "company.21.t"
	desc = "company.21.d"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	      NOT = {
					     owner = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
		  }
	      OR = {  #Minimum CD
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd } }
				owner = { 
						had_country_flag = {
						    flag = trade_company_spread_cd
							days = 30
						}
                }					
		  }
		  OR = {
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
		 }
		 OR = {
					         AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = india_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = indochina_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = china_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50

###Trading Company Upgrade(Hidden)
province_event = {
    id = company.211
	title = "company.21.t"
	desc = "company.21.d"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
			  
	      owner = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
	 
	      OR = {  #Minimum CD
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd } }
				owner = { 
						had_country_flag = {
						    flag = trade_company_spread_cd
							days = 30
						}
                }					
		  }
		  OR = {
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
		 }
		 OR = {
					         AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = india_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50

###Trading Company Degrade/Shrink
province_event = {
    id = company.22
	title = "company.22.t"
	desc = "company.22.d"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	      NOT = {
		        owner = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
		  }
	      OR = {  #Minimum CD
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd } }
				owner = { 
						had_country_flag = {
						    flag = trade_company_spread_cd
							days = 30
						}
                }					
		  }
		  OR = {
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
		 }
		 OR = {
					        AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = india_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = indochina_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = china_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = persia_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = west_europe_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = west_mediterraneansea_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = west_mediterraneansea_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = central_europe_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = balticsea_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = balticsea_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = eastern_europe_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = tartary_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = tartary_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 NOT = { owner = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 0 } } }
                                             has_province_flag = near_east_company_local
							}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	              months = 1
	}
	option = {
	          name = company.22.a
	          trigger = { 
			            owner = { treasury = 50 } 
			            OR = {

###Trading Company Degrade/Shrink(Hidden)
province_event = {
    id = company.221
	title = "company.22.t"
	desc = "company.22.d"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
			  
	      owner = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
	 
	      OR = {  #Minimum CD
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd } }
				owner = { 
						had_country_flag = {
						    flag = trade_company_spread_cd
							days = 30
						}
                }					
		  }
		  OR = {
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4

			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_off_1
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_off_2
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_off_3
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					  clr_province_flag = india_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = indochina_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = china_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = persia_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = west_europe_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = west_mediterraneansea_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = central_europe_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = balticsea_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = eastern_europe_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = tartary_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = near_east_company_local

			  }
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_pri_1
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_pri_2
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_pri_3
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
	}

#Trading Company Yearly Calculation(Hidden)
country_event = {
    id = company.30
	title = "company.30.t"
	desc = "company.30.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
    hidden = yes
    trigger = {
	           NOT = { has_country_flag = trade_company_calculation_reveal }
	           OR = {
                    has_country_flag = india_private_company
                    has_country_flag = india_official_company
                    has_country_flag = indochina_official_company
                    has_country_flag = indochina_private_company
                    has_country_flag = indonesia_private_company
                    has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
                    has_country_flag = china_private_company
                    has_country_flag = china_official_company
                    has_country_flag = japan_korea_private_company
                    has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
                    has_country_flag = persia_private_company
                    has_country_flag = persia_official_company
                    has_country_flag = south_africa_private_company
                    has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
                    has_country_flag = east_africa_private_company
                    has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
                    has_country_flag = west_africa_private_company
                    has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
                    has_country_flag = west_europe_official_company
                    has_country_flag = west_europe_private_company
                    has_country_flag = west_mediterraneansea_official_company
                    has_country_flag = west_mediterraneansea_private_company
                    has_country_flag = central_europe_official_company
                    has_country_flag = central_europe_private_company
                    has_country_flag = balticsea_official_company
                    has_country_flag = balticsea_private_company
                    has_country_flag = eastern_europe_official_company
                    has_country_flag = eastern_europe_private_company
                    has_country_flag = tartary_official_company
                    has_country_flag = tartary_private_company
                    has_country_flag = near_east_official_company
                    has_country_flag = near_east_private_company
                }
                is_month = 1
                OR = {
				       NOT = { has_country_flag = trade_company_calculation }
				       had_country_flag = {
					                   flag = trade_company_calculation
					                   days = 335 #prevent accumulated delay
					   }
				}				
	}	
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	        days = 1
				
	}
	immediate = {
	    hidden_effect = {
		    clr_country_flag = trade_company_calculation  #Refresh Timer
	        set_country_flag = trade_company_calculation
	        if = {
			        limit = { 
                              OR = {
							         has_country_flag = india_private_company
									 has_country_flag = india_official_company
							  }
					}
					set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_expense value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_income value = 0 } 
					set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_balance value = 0 } 
                    set_variable = { which = india_company_size value = 0 }					
			        every_owned_province = {
					          limit = {
							            has_province_flag = india_company_local
										OR = {
										        has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
										}
							  }
							  #First Calculate Maintanance
							  owner = { set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 }		  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    OR = {
			                             has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
                                         has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier_2
                                         has_province_modifier = inland_center_of_trade_modifier
									     has_province_modifier = important_natural_harbor
									     has_province_modifier = river_estuary_modifier
		                                } 
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = marketplace
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = trade_depot
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = stock_exchange
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.9 } }
							  }

							         limit = { 
									    NOT = { development = 6 }

												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
										}
							  }
							  #First Calculate Maintanance
							  owner = { set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 }			  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    OR = {
			                             has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
                                         has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier_2
                                         has_province_modifier = inland_center_of_trade_modifier
									     has_province_modifier = important_natural_harbor
									     has_province_modifier = river_estuary_modifier
		                                } 
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = marketplace
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = trade_depot
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = stock_exchange
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.9 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    NOT = { development = 6 }
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = -0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    development = 9
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = {

									 }

							  }
							  if = {

									    development = 15

							  }
							  if = {

									    development = 18
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    development = 21
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = {

									    development = 24
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }

												      has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
										        }
							         } 
									 owner = { multiply_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 2 }
                                               change_variable = { which = near_east_company_size value = 1 }									 }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = {
									            OR = {
										              has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
												      has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
										        }
							         } 
									 owner = { multiply_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 3 }
                                               change_variable = { which = near_east_company_size value = 2 }									 }
							  }

									            OR = {
										              has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
												      has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
										        }
							         } 
									 owner = { multiply_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 4 }
                                               change_variable = { which = near_east_company_size value = 3 }									 }
							  }
							  if = {
							        limit = { owner = { trade_ideas = 7 } }
							        owner = { multiply_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_expense value = 0.9 } }
							  }
							  #Second,calculate income
							  owner = { set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0 } }
							  if = {

                                                OR = {
										              has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
												      has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
													  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
												      has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4

							        }

									    }

									    }

							        }

									          base_tax = 10
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.4 } } #80% Tax efficiency
							        }
									if = { 
							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 1
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }
									if = { 
							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 2
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }
									if = { 
							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 3
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }
									if = { 
							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 4
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }

									    }

									    }

							        }

									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }

							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 8
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }
									if = { 
							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 9
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }
									if = { 
							            limit = { 
									          base_production = 10
									    } 
									    owner = { change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_income value = 0.3 } }  #60% production efficiency
							        }

								}
							    #Third,calculate the result
								owner = {  
									          
							            set_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_balance which = near_east_company_cash_income } 
							            subtract_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_balance which = near_east_company_cash_expense } 
									
									    #Add the result to total
									    change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_total_income which = near_east_company_cash_income } 
									    change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_total_expense which = near_east_company_cash_expense } 
									    change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash_total_balance which = near_east_company_cash_balance } 
									
								}    
							  }
						      change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash which = near_east_company_cash_balance } 
							  #Automatic Funding
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -200 } }
											  treasury = 300
									}
									add_treasury = -300
									change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 300 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -150 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -200 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 300 }
											  }
											  treasury = 250
									}
									add_treasury = -250
									change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 250 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -100 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -150 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 250 }
											  }
											  treasury = 200
									}
									add_treasury = -200
									change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 200 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -50 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -100 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 200 }
											  }
											  treasury = 150
									}
									add_treasury = -150
									change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 150 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 0 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = -50 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 100 }
											  }
											  treasury = 100
									}
									add_treasury = -100
									change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 100 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 50 } }
											  treasury = 50
									}
									add_treasury = -50
									change_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 50 } 
							  }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	       name = "company.30.a"
	}
}

#Manage India Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.41
	title = "company.41.t"
	desc = "company.41.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.41.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = india_official_company
											 has_country_flag = india_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.411 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.41.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = india_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.412 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.41.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } } 
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.41.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.41.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.41.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.41.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.zt

#Fund India Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.411
	title = "company.411.t"
	desc = "company.411.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = india_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = india_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = india_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = india_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.india_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 100
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 200 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -100
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 100 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.india_cash_100_inc

							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 400 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -200
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.india_cash_200_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 500
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.india_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 1000
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10

#Manage indochina Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.42
	title = "company.42.t"
	desc = "company.42.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.42.a" 
                     trigger = {
								   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = indochina_official_company
											 has_country_flag = indochina_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.421 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.42.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = indochina_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.422 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.42.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.42.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.42 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.42.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.42.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.42 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.42.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.42.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.42 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.42.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.42.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.42 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.42.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.42.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = indochina_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.429 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.indonesia_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 100
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 200 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -100
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 100 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.indonesia_cash_100_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 200
                     name = "company.fund200" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 200
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 400 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -200
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.indonesia_cash_200_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 500
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.indonesia_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }

country_event = {
    id = company.432
	title = "company.432.t"
	desc = "company.432.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Draw 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = 50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = -50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.indonesia_cash_50
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Draw 100

#Manage china Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.44
	title = "company.44.t"
	desc = "company.44.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.44.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								           has_country_flag = china_official_company
										   has_country_flag = china_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.441 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.44.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = china_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.442 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.44.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.44.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = china_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = china_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.44 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.44.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.44.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.44 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.44.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.44.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = china_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = china_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.44 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.44.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.44.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = china_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = china_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = china_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.44 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.44.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.44.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = china_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.449 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }

        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.japan_korea_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100

                     }
                     ai_chance = {

							 modifier = {

							 }

                     add_treasury = -100
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 100 } }

country_event = {
    id = company.452
	title = "company.452.t"
	desc = "company.452.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Draw 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = 50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = -50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.japan_korea_cash_50
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Draw 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 100 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 400 } }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = 100
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = -100 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.japan_korea_cash_100
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Draw 200

                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 200 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 800 } }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = 200
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = -200 } }

                     ai_chance = {

                     add_treasury = 500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = -500 } }

#Manage persia Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.46
	title = "company.46.t"
	desc = "company.46.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.46.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								            has_country_flag = persia_official_company
											has_country_flag = persia_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.461 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.46.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = persia_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.462 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.46.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.46.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.46.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.46.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.46.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.46.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = persia_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.46.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.46.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = persia_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = persia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.46.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.46.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = persia_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.469 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund persia Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.461
	title = "company.461.t"
	desc = "company.461.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = persia_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = persia_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = persia_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = persia_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = persia_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }

        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.persia_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {

					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 100
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 200 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -100
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 100 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.west_africa_cash_100_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 200
                     name = "company.fund200" 
                     trigger = {

                     }
                     ai_chance = {

							 modifier = {

		             }
                     add_treasury = -200

					 custom_tooltip = company.west_africa_cash_200_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 500

country_event = {
    id = company.472
	title = "company.472.t"
	desc = "company.472.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Draw 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = 50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = -50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.west_africa_cash_50
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Draw 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 100 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0

							 }
		             }
