#Manage south_africa Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.48
	title = "company.48.t"
	desc = "company.48.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.48.a" 
                     trigger = {
								   OR = { 
								            has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
											has_country_flag = south_africa_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.481 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.48.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.482 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.48.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.48.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.48.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.48.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.48.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.48.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.48.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.48.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.48.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.48.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.489 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund south_africa Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.481
	title = "company.481.t"
	desc = "company.481.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = south_africa_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = south_africa_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = south_africa_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = south_africa_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					          
        }

        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.south_africa_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {

                     ai_chance = {

								   NOT = { treasury = 200 }
							 }

#Manage west_europe Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.61
	title = "company.61.t"
	desc = "company.61.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.61.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = west_europe_official_company
											 has_country_flag = west_europe_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.611 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.61.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = west_europe_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.612 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.61.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.61.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.61 } } 
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.61.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.61.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.61 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.61.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.61.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.61 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.61.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.61.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = west_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.61 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.61.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.61.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = west_europe_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.619 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund west_europe Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.611
	title = "company.611.t"
	desc = "company.611.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = west_europe_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = west_europe_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = west_europe_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.61 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = west_europe_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = west_europe_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.61 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_europe_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50

					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.62 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 200
                     name = "company.fund200" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 200
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 400 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -200
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = west_mediterraneansea_company_cash value = 200 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.west_mediterraneansea_cash_200_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.62 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 500
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {

								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = west_mediterraneansea_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.west_mediterraneansea_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.62 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 1000
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -1000
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = west_mediterraneansea_company_cash value = 1000 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.west_mediterraneansea_cash_1000_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.62 } }

    id = company.622

	desc = "company.622.d"

                     name = "company.fund50"

								   check_variable = { which = west_mediterraneansea_company_cash value = 50 }

								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_mediterraneansea_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }

#Manage central_europe Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.63
	title = "company.63.t"
	desc = "company.63.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.63.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = central_europe_official_company
											 has_country_flag = central_europe_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.631 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.63.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = central_europe_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.632 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.63.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.63.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } } 
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.63.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.63.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.63.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.63.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.63.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.63.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = central_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.63.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.63.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = central_europe_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.639 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund central_europe Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.631
	title = "company.631.t"
	desc = "company.631.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = central_europe_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = central_europe_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = central_europe_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = central_europe_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = central_europe_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = central_europe_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.central_europe_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.63 } }
        }

		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 400 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -200
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = balticsea_company_cash value = 200 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.balticsea_cash_200_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.64 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 500
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = balticsea_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.balticsea_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.64 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 1000
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -1000
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = balticsea_company_cash value = 1000 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.balticsea_cash_1000_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.64 } }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.64 } }
        }

#Manage eastern_europe Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.65
	title = "company.65.t"
	desc = "company.65.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.65.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = eastern_europe_official_company
											 has_country_flag = eastern_europe_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.651 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.65.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = eastern_europe_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.652 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.65.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.65.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } } 
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.65.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.65.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.65.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.65.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.65.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.65.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.65.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.65.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = eastern_europe_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.659 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund eastern_europe Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.651
	title = "company.651.t"
	desc = "company.651.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = eastern_europe_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = eastern_europe_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = eastern_europe_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.eastern_europe_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.65 } }

								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = tartary_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.tartary_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.66 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 1000
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -1000
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = tartary_company_cash value = 1000 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.tartary_cash_1000_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.66 } }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.66 } }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Manage near_east Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.67
	title = "company.67.t"
	desc = "company.67.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.67.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = near_east_official_company
											 has_country_flag = near_east_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.671 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.67.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = near_east_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.672 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.67.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.67.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.67 } } 
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.67.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.67.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.67 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.67.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.67.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.67 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.67.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.67.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = near_east_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.67 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.67.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.67.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = near_east_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.679 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund near_east Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.671
	title = "company.671.t"
	desc = "company.671.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = near_east_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.67 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = near_east_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.67 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = near_east_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50

#India Trading Company go bankrupt
country_event = {
    id = company.51
	title = "company.51.t"
	desc = "company.51.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	        has_country_flag = india_company
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 0 } }
			NOT = {
			        any_owned_province = {
					          AND = {
							        has_province_flag = india_company_local
							        OR = {  #Additional check in case of conquered provinces
									      has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
									}
							  }
					}
			}
	}

    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a" 
			add_prestige = -10
            clr_country_flag = india_company
			clr_country_flag = india_official_company
			clr_country_flag = india_private_company
			hidden_effect = {
			        change_variable = { which = num_of_tc value = -1 }
			        every_owned_province = {
					          limit = {
							        has_province_flag = india_company_local
							  }
							  clr_province_flag = india_company_local
					}
			}
    }
}

	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	        has_country_flag = persia_company
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 0 } }
			NOT = {
			        any_owned_province = {
					          AND = {
							        has_province_flag = persia_company_local
							        OR = {  #Additional check in case of conquered provinces
									      has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
									}
							  }
					}
			}
	}

    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a" 
			add_prestige = -10
            clr_country_flag = persia_company
			clr_country_flag = persia_official_company
			clr_country_flag = persia_private_company
			hidden_effect = {
			        change_variable = { which = num_of_tc value = -1 }
			        every_owned_province = {
					          limit = {
							        has_province_flag = persia_company_local
							  }
							  clr_province_flag = persia_company_local
					}
			}
    }
}

#Moving capital to the same superregion will remove trading company
province_event = {
    id = company.60
	title = "company.60.t"
	desc = "company.60.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = india_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = india_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = east_indies_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = east_indies_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = indo_china_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = indo_china_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = china_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = china_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = west_europe_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = west_europe_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = west_mediterraneansea_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = west_mediterraneansea_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = central_europe_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = central_europe_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = north_europe_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = north_europe_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = eastern_europe_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = eastern_europe_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = inner_asia_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = inner_asia_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = far_east_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = far_east_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = west_africa_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = west_africa_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = eastern_africa_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = eastern_africa_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = southern_africa_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = southern_africa_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = near_east_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = near_east_superregion
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						superregion = middle_east_superregion
					}
				}
				superregion = middle_east_superregion
			}
		}		
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_province_flag = india_company_local
				has_province_flag = indochina_company_local
				has_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
				has_province_flag = china_company_local
				has_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
				has_province_flag = persia_company_local
				has_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
				has_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
				has_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
				has_province_flag = west_europe_company_local
				has_province_flag = west_mediterraneansea_company_local
				has_province_flag = central_europe_company_local
				has_province_flag = balticsea_company_local
				has_province_flag = eastern_europe_company_local
				has_province_flag = tartary_company_local
				has_province_flag = near_east_company_local

			}        
			OR = {  #Additional check in case of conquered provinces
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
				has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
	}
	immediate = {
		clr_province_flag = india_company_local
		clr_province_flag = indochina_company_local
		clr_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
		clr_province_flag = china_company_local
		clr_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
		clr_province_flag = persia_company_local
		clr_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
		clr_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
		clr_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
		clr_province_flag = west_europe_company_local
		clr_province_flag = west_mediterraneansea_company_local
		clr_province_flag = central_europe_company_local
		clr_province_flag = balticsea_company_local
		clr_province_flag = eastern_europe_company_local
		clr_province_flag = tartary_company_local
		clr_province_flag = near_east_company_local 
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
		remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
	}

    option = { #Dust to dust.
		name = "company.5.a"
	}
}

#If official trading company and private trading company appear in the same province, remove the private one.
province_event = {
    id = company.71
	title = "company.71.t"
	desc = "company.71.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {				
				AND = {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
						}        
						OR = {							
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
						}
				}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 1
	}
	immediate = {
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
	}
	
    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a"
    }
}
